Hey Moriah, I know your probably never going to see this but I really wanted to thank you.  I got your create this book 2 a few years back when I was still young, and it was the first time I ever tried at art, it was the thing that got my passion ignited. I specifically remember doing the page where it said to combine two animals into one, and it was the first drawing I ever did with a pencil outline before the actual outline, and it was the first drawing I did where I actually tried and it changed EVERYTHING. I know it probably was rough at the time, but I remember being so proud of this little drawing I did. Now I've been steadily improving my art, and I've found it's one of my true passions, its one of things that makes me who I am. I love art, everything about it. It was the same thing with the tools, I never would have thought to get colored pencils, or poscas, or a good sketchbook, but I watched you do those things in your videos, and looked up to the art you do, and my art was made a hundred times better by it.  I never would've found my passion for art if it wasn't for your book, and your videos. You've changed my life. And Even if I don't watch your videos as much anymore I will never stop being thankful for you. So I just had to say thank you â¤
